A dance instructor gives you tools‚Äîtools on how to take something and make it yours. It‚Äôs up to you how you make it yours, unique, great. We‚Äôre all human, and might not always live up to our own impossible expectations. All we can do is our best in the moment, and make choices. I choose to always see the positive, the silver lining. Dance is my therapy, my escape. If work, chores, bills, and family drama have me down, my dance lesson lets me turn off all the stress and focus on something fun, challenging and rewarding. <user_id>112151672897783294805< /user_id><Name>Maria Villarreal< /Name><Time>1529802213603< /Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I am pleased to say that since Lucas got involved with the Fox Studio, this venue has become an excellent place where to learn how to dance.  The teachers are very well trained in what seems to be a short period of time, and they are proficient instructing students through private lessons as well as group lessons; and, It is amazing to see how well adapted they are to work with children, teens and adults.

A BIG PLUS at the Fox is that people who like to dance can choose from so many styles:  from Ballroom to Belly Dancing, to Adult Ballet, to Tap, to Specialty Dances such as Argentine Tango, the choice is yours!  Another big plus is that I never feel pushed into anything.  All they offer is there to be seen, and it is up to me to decide whether to add a new challenge to my dancing.  Last but not least, the Coaches invited to the Fox Studio are simply World Class!

Maria Villarreal<//text>

I rerouted a mid size/weight package to this UPS store because signature was required. When I picked up the package, the representative set it on the counter and asked me to overreaching for it because she said it's their policy for social distancing. I understand we are in a pandemic but overreaching for heavy items can cause physical injuries. Why cant they just install a flex plastic like the supermarket? Even their credit machine needs one to fully extended the arm to sign. So many ways to social distance than having customers overreaching to pay and to get packages. Not only it's not effective (my arms aren't 6ft), it's physically inconvenient and challenge. So many restaurants set up a separate table for the take outs. UPS store can do the same. I will go to a different UPS store from now on.< /Review>

< review>
I went in on Monday to have a document notarized. Upon arriving, I noticed the notary was just finishing with other customers. I let him know at that time that I would also need a document notarized and he said " I can do it really quick," and waved me over.

He then started asking me where I needed to sign and where he needed to notarize. I myself am not a notary and thought that he would actually READ THE DOCUMENTS he was notarizing. Sensing his urgency, I glanced quickly over the document and we agreed together where he should notorize and I should sign. He was in such a rush to leave he was  out the door before I had even completed paying for the service.

So then I went home to prepare the documents for mailing and noticed that there was a notary field not filled out on the document. Not clear to me what the difference is between that and the other one that was filled out but went back in the hopes that I could just have it filled out, for peace of mind.

I went back today, Wednesday, and was told by another notary that what was filled out "should be enough." He wad unable to say with certainty that it was enough though. I explained that I would like it filled out completely and he said that he could notarize it for AN ADDITIONAL 10 DOLLARS! SERIOUSLY?! I paid for the service AGAIN because I wanted the peace of mind but HORRIBLE, CRAPPY CUSTOMER SERVICE!

I recommend taking your business elsewhere if you would like the notary to do a thorough job. Also, it is pretty clear that they are just out to make a quick buck here, and not necessarily maintain loyal customers.<//review>

<date>1448481765034</date><Rating>4<//Rating><text>Thien An may be the only place I've experienced 7 Course Beef before, but it set the bar pretty high. The best tip I can give is to go with someone who knows their stuff. Several visits later, I still haven't learned the art of wrapping a spring roll. Most of my friends just give up and end up making a "spring taco."

At $16.99 per order, don't expect to be overwhelmed with meat, but you'd be surprised how full you'll be after all 7 courses. We usually split an order of 7 course beef and a bun cha gio (vermicelli topped with egg rolls) between two people, and leave feeling stuffed. Feel free to order more rice paper, but vermicelli is an extra charge.

Finally gathered enough people to try the catfish recently, and that was rather disappointing. We ordered the large size catfish at about $50, and I just didn't think it was worth it. For a little more, I could have enjoyed a lobster from Newport Tan Cang Seafood!

Beware of the wait for dinner on weekends (make a reservation!). You know those Asian families love to get together and fight for the check!< /text>< pics>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
Great place and very affordable. Dollar General carries everything from clothing to groceries. The employees are very friendly and this time I went with my mom it was not full. No long wait times to pay either. One thing I do notice evertime I go, they are always over stocked with clothing inventory. They need to better organize the clothing to not make it appear cluttered. The clothing is located in the front center of the store and looks messy. Some aisles  have many boxes of merchandise in the way, which makes it hard to walk down aisles. With that said the prices and friendliness of the employees outweighs that.< /Text>
